# Comments for Question 4, LLM=Qwen QwQ-32B 16K

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.5)
    The story effectively uses symbolism (hexagons representing unity) and creates meaningful subtext about keeping promises and second chances. The monster as embodiment of "collective failure to keep our word" elevates the narrative beyond a simple monster story. The ending provides satisfying closure while suggesting continued growth. However, the emotional impact is somewhat diluted by telling rather than showing in key moments, and some metaphors ("like overgrown toddlers") feel more clever than resonant.

  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=7.5)
    The story effectively uses the seashell as a symbol for self-reflection, with the mirror imagery creating layers of meaning about self-acceptance. The theme of facing one's true self to break free from self-imposed limitations resonates emotionally. However, the conflict resolves too neatly, with insufficient tension before the breakthrough moment.

  * grade_story_107.txt (grade=7.9)
    The story effectively employs symbolism through the typewriter as knowledge-keeper and the crystal ball as truth-revealer. The central theme of redemption through honesty emerges organically from the narrative. The ending delivers emotional impact by subverting expectations—Ernest's victory comes not through revenge but through accepting responsibility. The writing shows restraint in emotional moments, allowing readers to connect with Ernest's transformation. However, the conflict resolution relies somewhat on convenient timing rather than character agency.

  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=7.5)
    The story effectively uses symbolism (mirrors, reef, lighthouse) to explore themes of regret, atonement, and impossible choices. The emotional impact is strong, particularly in the knight's final acceptance of his humanity. However, the story occasionally tells rather than shows emotional states, and some metaphors feel slightly overwrought. The central conflict and resolution are clear, though the transformation from physical quest to spiritual atonement could be more subtly rendered.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=8.7)

The subtext about memory, identity, and rebirth adds meaningful depth, but some metaphors ("bound with starlight") verge on being too abstract.
